Supreme Court of the United States isthe only court mandated by the
stitution and is the court of last resort. The Supreme Court has original
diction over all disputes involving foreign ministers and interstate
tes, and disputes between the federal and state governments. The .
Court bas jurisdiction of cases originating from any other court if the case
involves constitutional issues, federal laws or maritime treaties and laws.
‘ha Supreme Court may affirm, modify, reverse or remand a decision of a
ower court. The Supreme Court is comprised of the Chief Justice and
associate justices, who are appointed by the President and confirmed
by. ¢ Senate. Among his or her responsibilities, each Justice is assigned
& serve as “Circuit Justice” for one or more of the United States Judicial

United States Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit 7

 

ited States Courts of
jpeals

termediate appellate courts in the federal judicial system are the
cof appeals. Twelve of these courts have jurisdiction over cases from
geographic, areas. The Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit has
‘al jurisdiction over specific types of cases, A disappointed party in a
Hct court usually has the right to- have the case reviewed in the court of
cals for the circuit. Appeals court judges are appointed for life by the
‘dent with the advice and consent of the Senate. Each court of appeals
gists of six ot More judges, depending on the caseload of the court. The
é who has served on the court the longest and who is under 65 years
26 is designated as the chief judge and performs administrative duties
ddition to hearing cases. , .

nited States Court of Appeals for
he Federal Circuit Dk

The United States Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit handles cases
: subject matter without regard to the region. The Court hears all appeals
for the United States Court of Federal Claims, the United States Court of
International Trade and the United States Court of Veterans Appeals. The
Federal Circuit hears appeals from United States District Courts in patent
‘Gases, cases involving energy regulation and economic stabilization as well
as appeals from a variety of administrative proceedings. Established in
982, the Washington, DC-based Federal Circuit possesses national
jurisdiction as a result of the merger between the Appellate Division of the
former United States Court of Clatms and the United States Court of
‘Customs and Patent Appeals.
